s.synced.delete(wa) {\n   168→\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n   169→\t\t\tbreak\n   170→\t\t} else if wa.ch == nil {\n   171→\t\t\t// already canceled (e.g., cancel/close race)\n   172→\t\t\tbreak\n   173→\t\t} else if wa.compacted {\n   174→\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n   175→\t\t\tbreak\n   176→\t\t}\n   177→\n   178→\t\tif !wa.victim {\n   179→\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   180→\t\t\tpanic(\"watcher not victim but not in watch groups\")\n   181→\t\t}\n   182→\n   183→\t\tvar victimBatch watcherBatch\n   184→\t\tfor _, wb := range s.victims {\n   185→\t\t\tif wb[wa] != nil {\n 193→\t\t\tdelete(victimBatch, wa)\n   194→\t\t\tbreak\n   195→\t\t}\n   196→\n   197→\t\t// victim being processed so not accessible; retry\n   198→\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   199→\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Millisecond)\n   200→\t}\n   201→\n   202→\twa.ch = nil\n   203→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   204→}\n   205→\n   206→func (s *watchableStore) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n in the unsynced map every 100ms.\n   223→func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchersLoop() {\n   224→\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n   225→\n   226→\tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\n   227→\tdefer 234→\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n   235→\n   236→\t\tunsyncedWatchers := 0\n   237→\t\tif lastUnsyncedWatchers > 0 {\n   238→\t\t\tunsyncedWatchers, evs = s.syncWatchers(evs)\n   239→\t\t}\n watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\n   259→func (s *watchableStore) syncVictimsLoop() {\n   260→\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n   261→\n   262→\tfor {\n   263→\t\tfor s.moveVictims() != 0 {\n   264→\t\t\t// try to update all victim watchers\n   265→\t\t}\n   266→\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n   267→\t\tisEmpty := len(s.victims) == 0\n   268→\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n   269→\n   270→\t\tvar tickc <-chan *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\n   286→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   287→\tvictims := s.victims\n   288→\ts.victims = nil\n   289→\ts.mu.Unlock()\n   290→\n   291→\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\n   292→\tfor _, wb := range victims {\n   293→\t\t// try to send responses again\n   294→\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n   295→\t\t\t// watcher has observed the store up to, but not including, w.minRev\n   296→\t\t\trev := w.minRev - 1\n   297→\t\t\tif !w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n   298→\t\t\t\tif newVictim == nil {\n   299→\t\t\t\t\tnewVictim = 340→\n   341→// syncWatchers syncs unsynced watchers by:\n   342→//  1. choose a set of watchers from the unsynced watcher group\n   343→//  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\n   344→//  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\n   345→//  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\n   346→func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\n   347→\ts.mu.Lock()\n   348→\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n   349→\n   350→\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 370→\t\t\t// Skip the watcher that failed to send compacted watch response due to w.ch is full.\n   371→\t\t\t// Next retry of syncWatchers would try to resend the compacted watch response to w.ch\n   372→\t\t\tcontinue\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\tw.minRev = max(curRev+1, w.minRev)\n   375→\n   376→\t\teb, ok := wb[w]\n   377→\t\tif !ok {\n   378→\t\t\t// bring un-notified watcher to synced\n   388→\t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: curRev}) {\n   389→\t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n   390→\t\t} else {\n   391→\t\t\tw.victim = true\n 399→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n   402→\t\t}\n   403→\t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n   404→\t}\n   405→\ts.addVictim(victims)\n   406→\n   407→\tvsz := 0\n   408→\tfor 416→// rangeEventsWithReuse returns events in range [minRev, maxRev), while reusing already provided events.\n   417→func rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n   418→\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n   419→\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n   420→\t}\n   421→\t// append from left\n   422→\tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision > minRev {\n   423→\t\tevs = append(rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, evs[0].Kv.ModRevision), evs...)\n   424→\t}\n   425→\t// cut from left\n   426→\tprefixIndex := 0\n   427→\tfor prefixIndex < len(evs) && evs[prefixIndex].Kv.ModRevision < minRev {\n   428→\t\tprefixIndex++\n   429→\t}\n   430→\tevs = evs[prefixIndex:]\n   431→\n   432→\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n   433→\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n   434→\t}\n   435→\t// append from right\n   436→\tif evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1 < maxRev {\n   437→\t\tevs = append(evs, rangeEvents(lg, b, evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1, maxRev)...)\n   438→\t}\n   439→\t// cut from right\n   440→\tsuffixIndex := len(evs) - 1\n   441→\tfor suffixIndex >= 0 && evs[suffixIndex].Kv.ModRevision >= maxRev {\n   442→\t\tsuffixIndex--\n   443→\t}\n   444→\tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\n   445→\treturn evs\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→// rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\n   449→func rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n   450→\tif minRev < 0 {\n   451→\t\tlg.Warn(\"Unexpected negative revision range start\", zap.Int64(\"minRev\", minRev))\n   452→\t\tminRev = 0\n   453→\t}\n   454→\tminBytes, maxBytes := NewRevBytes(), NewRevBytes()\n   455→\tminBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: minRev}, minBytes)\n   456→\tmaxBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: maxRev}, maxBytes)\n   457→\n   458→\t// UnsafeRange returns keys and values. And in boltdb, keys are revisions.\n   459→\t// values are actual key-value pairs in backend.\n   460→\ttx := b.ReadTx()\n   461→\ttx.RLock()\n   462→\trevs, vs := tx.UnsafeRange(schema.Key, minBytes, maxBytes, 0)\n   463→\tevs := kvsToEvents(lg, revs, vs)\n   464→\t// Must unlock after kvsToEvents, because vs (come from boltdb memory) is not deep copy.\n   465→\t// We can only unlock after event at the given rev just happened to\n   491→// watchers that watch on the key of the event.\n   492→func (s *watchableStore) notify(rev int64, evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n   493→\tvictim := wa.minRev {\n\t\t\twa.minRev = startRev\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.synced.add(wa)\n\t} else {\n\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Inc()\n\t\ts.unsynced.add(wa)\n\t}\n\ts.revMu.RUnlock()\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\twatcherGauge.Inc()\n\n\treturn wa, func() { s.cancelWatcher(wa) }\n}\n\n// cancelWatcher removes references of the watcher from the watchableStore\nfunc (s *watchableStore) cancelWatcher(wa *watcher) {\n\tfor {\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\tif s.unsynced.delete(wa) {\n\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if s.synced.delete(wa) {\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if wa.ch == nil {\n\t\t\t// already canceled (e.g., cancel/close race)\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t} else if wa.compacted {\n\t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif !wa.victim {\n\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\tpanic(\"watcher not processed so not accessible; retry\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\t\ttime.Sleep(time.Millisecond)\n\t}\n\n\twa.ch = nil\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n}\n\nfunc (s *watchableStore) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\terr := s.store.Restore(b)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tfor wa := range s.synced.watchers {\n\t\twa.restore = syncWatchersLoop() {\n\tdefer s.wg.Done()\n\n\tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\n\tdefer delayTicker.Stop()\n\tvar evs []mvccpb.Event\n\n\tfor {\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\tst := unsyncedWatchers {\n\t\t\t// be fair to other store operations by yielding time taken\n\t\t\tdelayTicker.Reset(syncDuration)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\n\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// syncVictimsLoop tries to write precomputed watcher responses to\n// watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\nfunc (s *watchableStore) 0\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tvar tickc <-chan time.Time\n\t\tif !isEmpty {\n\t\t\ttickc = time.After(10 * time.Millisecond)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-tickc:\n\t\tcase <-s.victimc:\n\t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// moveVictims tries to update watches with already pending event data\nfunc (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tvictims := s.victims\n\ts.victims = nil\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\n\tfor _, wb := range victims {\n\t\t// try to send responses again\n\t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n\t\t\t// watcher has the unsynced watcher group\n//  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\n//  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\n//  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\nfunc (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\n\t}\n\n\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced s.store.compactMainRev\n\n\twg, minRev := s.unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)\n\tevs = rangeEventsWithReuse(s.store.lg, s.store.b, evs, minRev, curRev+1)\n\n\tvictims := provided events.\nfunc rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n\tif len(evs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n\t}\n\t// append from left\n\tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision > minRev {\n\t\tevs = append(rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, evs[0].Kv.ModRevision), evs...)\n\t}\n\t// cut from left\n\tprefixIndex := returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\nfunc rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n\tif minRev < 0 {\n\t\tlg.Warn(\"Unexpected negative revision RevToBytes(Revision{Main: maxRev}, maxBytes)\n\n\t// UnsafeRange returns keys and values. And in boltdb, keys are revisions.\n\t// values are actual key-value pairs in backend.\n\ttx := b.ReadTx()\n\ttx.RLock()\n\trevs, vs := tx.UnsafeRange(schema.Key, minBytes, maxBytes, 0)\n\tevs := we will trigger SIGSEGV during boltdb re-mmap.\n\ttx.RUnlock()\n\treturn evs\n}\n\n// kvsToEvents gets all events for the watchers from all key-value pairs\nfunc kvsToEvents(lg *zap.Logger, revs, vals watchers that watch on the key of the event.\nfunc (s *watchableStore) notify(rev int64, evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n\tvictim := make(watcherBatch)\n\tfor w, eb := range newWatcherBatch(&s.synced, evs) Compaction happens every 5 minutes.\ntype Revision struct {\n\tlg *zap.Logger\n\n\tclock     clockwork.Clock\n\tretention int64\n\n\trg RevGetter\n\tc  Compactable\n\n\tctx    context.Context\n\tcancel context.CancelFunc\n\n\tmu     sync.Mutex\n\tpaused bool\n}\n\n// newRevision creates a new instance of Revisonal compactor that purges\n// the log older than retention revisions from the current revision.\nfunc newRevision(lg *zap.Logger, clock clockwork.Clock, retention int64, rg RevGetter, c Compactable) *Revision {\n\trc := &Revision{\n\t\tlg:        lg,\n\t\tclock:     clock,\n\t\tretention: retention,\n\t\trg:        rg,\n\t\tc:         c,\n\t}\n\trc.ctx, rc.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\treturn rc\n}\n\nconst revInterval = 5 * time.Minute\n\n// Run runs revision-based compactor.\nfunc (rc *Revision) Run() {\n\tprev := int64(0)\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tfor {\n\t\t\tselect {\n\t\t\tcase <-rc.ctx.Done():\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\tcase <-rc.clock.After(revInterval):\n\t\t\t\trc.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tp := rc.paused\n\t\t\t\trc.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tif p {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\trev := rc.rg.Rev() - rc.retention\n\t\t\tif rev <= 0 || rev == prev {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tnow := time.Now()\n\t\t\trc.lg.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\"starting auto revision compaction\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision-compaction-retention\", rc.retention),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t_, err := rc.c.Compact(rc.ctx, &pb.CompactionRequest{Revision: rev})\n\t\t\tif err == nil || errors.Is(err, mvcc.ErrCompacted) {\n\t\t\t\tprev = rev\n\t\t\t\trc.lg.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\t\"completed auto revision compaction\",\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision-compaction-retention\", rc.retention),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"took\", time.Since(now)),\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\trc.lg.Warn(\n\t\t\t\t\t\"failed auto revision compaction\",\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision-compaction-retention\", rc.retention),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"retry-interval\", revInterval),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n\n// Stop stops revision-based compactor.\nfunc (rc *Revision) Stop() {\n\trc.cancel()\n}\n\n// Pause pauses revision-based compactor.\nfunc (rc *Revision) Pause() {\n\trc.mu.Lock()\n\trc.paused = true\n\trc.mu.Unlock()\n}\n\n// Resume resumes revision-based compactor.\nfunc (rc *Revision) Resume() {\n\trc.mu.Lock()\n\trc.paused = false\n\trc.mu.Unlock()\n}\n","numLines":132,"startLine":1,"totalLines":132}}}

through multiple components that work together to manage historical versions and notify affected watch streams:\\n\\n## Compaction Scheduling\\n\\nCompaction is scheduled through two mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **Periodic Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go`): The `Periodic` type implements time-based compaction, recording revisions at regular intervals (1/10th of the retention period) and executing compaction when the retention period expires. The `Run()` method starts a background goroutine that periodically invokes `Compact()`.\\n\\n2. **Revision-Based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go`): The `Revision` type implements compaction based on revision count, compacting every 5 minutes to remove revisions older than a specified retention count. Both schedulers use the `Compactable` interface to call the actual compaction logic.\\n\\n## Compaction Modes\\n\\nThe main compactor interface is defined in `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go`. The `New()` factory function selects either `ModePeriodic` or `ModeRevision` based on configuration, providing a unified `Compactor` interface with `Run()`, `Stop()`, `Pause()`, and `Resume()` methods.\\n\\n## Compaction Execution\\n\\nWhen compaction is triggered:\\n\\n1. **RPC Handler** (`server/etcdserver/v3_server.go`): The `Compact()` method receives a `CompactionRequest` and routes it through the Raft consensus layer for consistency.\\n\\n2. **Apply Layer** (`server/etcdserver/apply/backend.go`): The `Compaction()` method handles applying the compaction to the backend store via `KV.Compact()`.\\n\\n3. **Store Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go`): The `Compact()` method is the main entry point that:\\n   - Checks if the previous compaction completed using `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()`\\n   - Updates the compact revision via `updateCompactRev()`\\n   - Schedules the actual compaction job via `compact()` method, which runs asynchronously using a FIFO scheduler\\n\\n4. **Scheduled Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go`): The `scheduleCompaction()` method executes the compaction in batches:\\n   - Calls `kvindex.Compact()` to compact the index\\n   - Iterates through key-value revisions in batches (controlled by `CompactionBatchLimit`)\\n   - Deletes revisions that are not in the \\\"keep\\\" map (computed by the index compaction)\\n   - Computes a hash for verification purposes\\n   - Updates `FinishedCompact` marker in the backend\\n\\n## Index Compaction\\n\\n1. **Tree Index** (`server/storage/mvcc/index.go`): The `Compact()` method compacts the tree index by:\\n   - Cloning the B-tree to avoid locking during compaction\\n   - Calling `keyIndex.compact()` on each key to remove superseded versions\\n   - Deleting empty key indices\\n   - Returning a map of available revisions to keep\\n\\n2. **Key Index** (`server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go`): The `doCompact()` method:\\n   - Walks through generations of a key's versions\\n   - Marks the first revision <= compaction revision as available\\n   - Removes older generations and versions\\n   - Updates `keep` map for revisions that must be retained\\n\\n## Watch Stream State Management\\n\\n**Watch Streams** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher.go`): The `WatchStream` interface manages watch requests. The `WatchResponse` struct includes a `CompactRevision` field set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction.\\n\\n## Compaction Notification to Watchers\\n\\nWhen a watch stream's requested revision is compacted, it must be notified immediately:\\n\\n1. **Watchable Store** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`): \\n   - Maintains separate groups of synced and unsynced watchers\\n   - The `syncWatchers()` method syncs unsynced watchers by reading historical events\\n   - Calls `wg.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactRev)` to select watchers to sync\\n\\n2. **Watcher Group** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go`): The `chooseAll()` method is critical for compaction notification:\\n   - Iterates through selected watchers\\n   - For each watcher with `minRev < compactRev`: sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision` set to the compaction revision\\n   - Sets `watcher.compacted = true` to mark it as cancelled\\n   - Deletes the watcher from the group\\n   - If the watcher's channel is full (blocked), retries on the next sync\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection\\n\\n**Slow Watchers** are watches that fall behind the current revision due to slow event processing:\\n\\n1. **Detection** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`): The `watch()` method determines if a watcher is slow:\\n   - If `startRev > currentRev` or `startRev == 0`: watcher is synced, added to `synced` group\\n   - If `startRev <= currentRev`: watcher is unsynced, added to `unsynced` group, increments `slowWatcherGauge`\\n\\n2. **Victim Handling**: Watchers with blocked channels (victims) are moved to a `victims` list and periodically retried by `syncVictimsLoop()` and `moveVictims()`.\\n\\n3. **Metrics** (`server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`): The `slowWatcherGauge` tracks the total number of slow (unsynced) watchers. Additional metrics track compaction timing (`indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`).\\n\\n## State Persistence\\n\\n**Store Management** (`server/storage/mvcc/store.go`) maintains compaction state:\\n- `UnsafeReadFinishedCompact()`: Reads the last finished compaction revision from backend metadata\\n- `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact()`: Reads the scheduled compaction revision\\n- `UnsafeSetScheduledCompact()` / `UnsafeSetFinishedCompact()`: Persist compaction markers to enable recovery\\n\\n## Compaction-Watch Integration\\n\\nThe system ensures no watch gaps through:\\n- **Compaction-Aware Syncing**: `syncWatchers()` respects `compactMainRev` when selecting watchers to sync\\n- **Immediate Cancellation**: Watchers that span a compacted revision receive `CompactRevision` notification before attempting to sync\\n- **RPC Propagation** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go`): The Watch RPC handler checks if `CompactRevision != 0` and marks the watcher as cancelled in the gRPC response\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":264,"cache_read_input_tokens":61299,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":264},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"23af8136-1bed-4b2f-9dcd-1f2427bb980e","uuid":"ac32c30c-80cc-478a-bf6c-da3e30bad721"}
